\entry{to temper} {} {} {In his famous book, \emph{The Prince}, Machiavelli asked on which side of a scale containing one of two animals the challenge for a ruler ruling over people weighs most heavily according to a given situation. On one side, Machiavelli sets the fox. On the other side, the lion. The weaker of the two is supposed to represent \emph{cunning} without strength. The stronger of the two \emph{brute force} with intelligence.  According to Machiavelli, a prudent ruler must be adaptive, changing to new situations, as problems arise, acting as a fox "in order to recognize traps" and as a lion when he has no choice but to "frighten off wolves." Machiavelli argues that the lion, the one symbolizing strength over intelligence, "is defenseless against traps" while the fox, the one symbolizing cunning over brute force, "is defenseless against wolves" and other physical threats; an effective ruler draws on the necessary, though not mutually exclusive, attributes of these great beasts, to keep his crown. \newline \indent It would not be fair to dismiss Machiavelli's analogy outright for imprecision but no analogy escapes reality unscathed; Machiavelli's is no exception. What is a trap? Who lays traps? Who benefits from traps? Is there not room for a hunter? \footnote{In his unparalleled contribution to the study of being in the \emph{Metaphysics}, Aristotle, for instance, criticized Socrates' theory of the forms by virtue of the third man; if man is man by virtue of his participation in the form of man, a second form for participation is required. A third form relating the form for participation to that of the participant is thus required. The process continues ad infinitum. Socrates' theory of the forms thus becomes a wind egg. (c.f., \emph{Theaetetus} 161a) Is there no third man argument by which great philosophers like the Jewish monotheist, Aristotle, might make to undermine analogies like Machiavelli's? Is it not plausible to imagine a hunter behind the scenes of the fox and the lion? } \newline \indent It is clear that Machiavelli's understanding of the scales of beastliness or animality is nothing but to be contained in the eye of the \emph{arbiter elegantiarum}. An example is an elegant debate. A trap laid for the public, the two jaws of the foot piece, designed to catch the minds of readers, came in the form of a measure designed according to its counter-measure, the two corresponding momentanae.  \newline \indent The article published on April 12, 2024 by the \emph{New York Times} under the title "The Math on Ukraine Doesn't Add Up"  (the measure) was written so as to be a measure for its pre-existing counter-measure. Senator Roger Wicker's memo entitled, "Production is Deterrence," with a publication date on April 22nd, 2024 is the pre-existing counter-measure. With the measure before its counter-measure appearing sequentially, the Republican Senators, J. D. Vance and Roger Wicker, successfully tempered a trap for swaying American public opinion about "the math" on a range of issues related to Ukraine's war \textfrench{matÃ©riel} away from disapproval to support for funding. The math, which adds up in Senator Roger Wicker's memo, doesn't in J. D. Vance's article but publishing the latter before the former allows for latter to appear as a refutation. The refutation, however, was designed according to what was to be refuted well ahead of time. Senator Roger Wicker thus tempered V. D. Vance to publish his article before his memo.  \newline \indent Since the American public is never informed about the backroom discussions centering on or the creation, revision, or conversations with newspapers about, these documents, the sequential nature of forming the measure according to a pre-existing counter-measure is entirely concealed from the public's eyes, just like a hunter's trap is concealed from a fox's or lion's feet. Out of sight, out of mind. Machiavelli's analogy is thus a great starting point for identifying the humanistic aspects of governance. Why would any one have any need for speechless beasts when so much is clear from speech alone? \newline \indent  Passage of the funding sailed through the two houses of congress onto President Biden's lap in no time.\footnote{["US House approves 61bn in military aid for Ukraine after months of stalling," \emph{The Guardian}, April 20th, 2024]; ["What the US Congress passed to aid Ukraine, Israel and Taiwan," \emph{Reuters}, April 23rd, 2024]; ["US Congress passes Ukraine aid after months of delay," \emph{Reuters}, April 23rd, 2024] } While the Republicans passed funding for Ukraine's war \textfrench{matÃ©riel}, funding made no apparent difference, as the Ukraine failed to change the status quo ante on the battlefield in any noticeable way. None of the Ukrainian newspapers, such as the \emph{Kyiv Independent} or \textukrainian{\emph{Ğ£ĞºÑ€Ğ°Ñ—Ğ½ÑÑŒĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ´Ğ°}}, published articles, describing how the newly passed aid for Ukraine or its new war \textfrench{matÃ©riel} made much of a difference. \newline \indent The problem is neither the hunter nor the trap but the fact that for the most part the animals never really realize what being trapped truly means. The failure to realize one is trapped is related almost exclusively to the fact that trap's objective is less to trap than to reinforce entrapment. The design of opposites, the counter-measure for the measure, ensnares people into thinking that these opposed points of view are really an opposition. The fact of the matter is that beyond the symmetrically designed teeth on opposite ends of a trap is a far greater wonder to behold. It is logic.

\entry{trade surplus, China's} {} {} {During the second anniversary of the Ukraine war, China, the world's second largest economy, shocked the world in 2024 when it announced a surplus from trade exceeding 990 billion dollars, beating a previous record from 2022 (i.e., the first year of the Ukraine war). China, however, beat the 2024 record in 2025. China's trade surplus in 2025 exceeded 1.2 trillion dollars, despite Donald J Trump's tariffs.\footnote{China met Trump's threat to impose tariffs as high as 145 per cent on Chinese goods with its own levy on the export of rare earths; China's a dominant player in rare earths. Capable of monetizing the extraction of inaccessible elements, China's ability to process extracts for sale is unrivaled. The crisis led to a one-year truce after a summit in South Korea in October, 2025.} Tariffs imposed by President Trump on China accomplished little, causing Chinese exports to the United States to drop by nearly a fifth.\footnote{["Chinaâ€™s Trade Surplus Reaches a Record of Nearly $1 Trillion," \emph{New York Times} January 12th, 2025], ["Chinaâ€™s Trade Surplus Climbs Past $1 Trillion for First Time," \emph{New York Times}. December 7th, 2025], ["How China racked up a 1tn trade surplus," \emph{Financial Times}. December 11th, 2025], ["China blames US for trade imbalances as surplus hits record 1.2tn," \emph{Financial Times}. January 14th, 2026], ["China Announces Record Trade Surplus as Its Exports Flood World Markets," \emph{New York Times}. January 14th, 2026]} \newline \indent China's 2025 trade surplus stands in direct contrast to the U.S.'s trade deficit. In a first of its kind correlation, the U.S. trade deficit is more or less equivalent to China's trade surplus with neither country affecting the balance much at all. The correlation is a historic correlation in the history of economics. Never before in the history of mankind, let alone economics, have two rival economies, the first but with a trade deficit, the second but with a trade surplus, met at a single figure as high as the figure for 2025. Compounding the problem is that China's trade surplus in factory goods alone is much larger as a share of its economy than that of the United States immediately after World War II when most of the likely competitors were in ruins; it is also so during the early years of Worl War I when the United States peacefully churned out civilian goods while more than six European nations battled to transform the subversion of or more competitors into a stepping stone for its own global dominance. China's trade surplus in manufactured goods now exceeds a 10th of the country's entire economic output. The result has been the creation of millions of jobs in China with factory closures or layoffs in other countries like Germany. China's production of electric vehicles has shattered the German automotive industry. In the face of Chinese competition, Volkswagen, one of Germany's most iconic automotive brands, second only only to Toyota Motor in the number of cars it sells globally, closed a plant in Dresden after 24 years. Volkswagenâ€™s woes mirrored those of the German economy, which shrank in 2023 and 2024 and has been stagnant in 2025.\footnote{The situation with China thus highlights how the uneven results "a revolt of the forces of production" elicit for the world economy. In his book, \emph{Bolsheviki and World Peace}, Trotsky wrote how "World production revolts not only against the confusion produced by national and state divisions but also against the capitalist economic organization, which has now turned into barbarous disorganization and chaos." (1918) The increase in jobs in China led to the loss of jobs elsewhere. China's plans for its economy upbraided those of other economies, creating disorder. While one economy produces the largest trade surplus in history, another slumps. One economy's tariffs may have a negative impact on another but no positive impact on the one. ["Volkswagen May Close German Plants for First Time in Its History," \emph{New York Times} October 30th, 2024], ["Volkswagen to End Production at German Plant, a First in Company History," \emph{New York Times}. December 16th, 2025], ["Volkswagen Suffers More Than Rivals From Auto Industry Woes," \emph{New York Times} January 10th, 2026]} Statistics such as these indicate that for intents and purposes, the United States cannot meet or beat China's economy. It is a sign of the times that the correlation indicates the upward trajectory of China's economy against the downward trajectory of the United State's. \newline \indent The United States appears to be oblivious. While the United States is pouring hundreds of billions of dollars into what are nothing more than police State activities, China is outperforming the U.S. economically. \entry{Tolbukhin, Fyodor} {} {} {Fyodor Tolbukhin, born on June 16th, 1894, is the first liberator of the Crimea. During his service he earned the distinguished Knight's Order of Victory. Tolbukhin, wounded and concussed twice, received the Orders of Anna and Stanislav before he received a recommendation to attend the Imperial Russian Army's Oranienbaum Rifle Officer School, Located on the Gulf of Finland west of St. Petersburg, the Oranienbaum Rifle Officer School, whose graduating officers received FN 1905 pistols with a stamp on the right hand side of the slide with a set of crossed rifles, learned how to integrate the Maxim or Colt machine guns into the existing units of the Russian Imperial Army.\footnote{\textrussian{Ğ–ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»Ñ‘Ğ² Ğ’. \entry{Undergrowth} {} {} {During Ukraine's 'Spring' counteroffensive, which neither happened in 'Spring' nor amounted to an offensive,' the premier British intelligence service, the cream of the crop from Oxford, Cambridge, King's College London, and Sandhurst, issued an alarming report, accounting for Ukraine's mounting difficulties in overcoming the massive undergrowth characterizing the length of the line, the great Russian general, Surovikin, constructed during the battle of Bakhmut-Artemovsk. \newline \indent Published by her majesty's Defense Intelligence on August 3rd, 2023, the intelligence update manifested three bullet points. The first stated: "[undergrowth] regrowing across the battlefields of southern Ukraine is likely one factor contributing to the generally slow progress of combat in the area." The second stated: "[the] predominately arable land in the combat zone has now been left fallow for 18 months, with the return of weeds and shrubs accelerating under the warm, damp summer conditions. The extra cover helps camouflage Russian defensive positions and makes defensive mine fields harder to clear." The third stated "Although undergrowth can also provide cover for small stealthy infantry assaults, the net effect has been to make it harder for either side to make advances." 
}

\entry{unipolar moment} {} {} {China's unipolar moment occured slowly, without fanfare, a media sensation, or a major political event. China's rise to the World's Superpower happened gradually over time primarily due to its ability to exploit the weaknesses its own enemy exposed frequently, carelessly, or haphazardly. During the third stage in the destruction of America's superpower, beginning in 1973 but beginning in 1991, prepared the groundwork for most of the schemes China has exploited to develop societal, technological, cultural, or economic\footnote{} gains against the United States. During the period from 1991 to 2008 when the United States began to display the character of self-destruction more deeply than in the previous three stages stages, the United States became aware of China's rising might in all of its manifestation but simply ignored the warning signs. In the fifth period of America's lost superpower, the United States could not but watch as China began to benefit immensely from strengthening the results derived from the techniques America's own mismanagement of its exposed weaknesses provided. The fifth period of America's lost superpower is from 2008 to 2026 when America's currency as the world's global reserve currency subsided.\footnote{["Could the US dollar lose its reserve-currency status?" \emph{Allianz} June 6th, 2018], ["What if â€“ the US dollar loses its status as the worldâ€™s reserve currency?" \emph{Roland Berger}. Morgan} July 1st, 2025], ["The International Role of the U.S. Dollar," \emph{Board of Governors of the Federal Reserve System}. Hollywood, the home of America's cultural heritage, is ravished with its producers in chains, locked up, behind bars. Chicago, Illinois plays reruns of heroes from municipal services like Chicago PD, Ambulance, Fire, Paramedic. New York's new mayor, a politician just like the last, is manufactured precisely for consent with New York's ruling elites. California, the fourth largest economy in the world, contributed nothing but billions but none of the billions could help. The great State of Texas, a Lone Star, produced a year of the greatest output in oil but even with the greatest output of oil, the Gadsden snake, overladen with the baggage of hundreds of thousands of different types of ticks sucking blood from a heart living on Geitner's xerocopies, whimpered across the global finish line with a trillion in trade deficits for a Federal debt filled with trillions of dead Washingtons, Lincolns, Hamiltons, Jacksons or Benjamins. The great founders look on, dismayed. Treaded upon heavily, the country is now but a shallow reminiscience of a power no longer powerful.}

\entry{uranium} {} {} {During the Ukraine war, uranium\footnote{In a documentary produced under the auspices of the Bureau of Mines of the United States Department of the Interior called \emph{The Petrified River} (1957) on uranium mining in the West, the narrator provides a short, concise, straightforward explanation of uranium. It describes uranium thus: "For the elements that make our earth came from the fiery cores of ancient suns, billions of years ago. The simplest of all these elements is the hydrogen atom; it has a single proton in its nucleus and an electron that circles it like a planet. Within suns hydrogen atoms fuse together and are joined by two neutrons. The result is a completely new element, Helium, whose two protons attract a pair of circling electrons. Helium in turn becomes the next heaviest element, Lithium, as more particles join its nucleus. Thus one by one all the 92 elements were forged in stellar fire until the heaviest atom of all was, uranium, was created. Uranium, with a nucleus of 92 protons and nearly twice as many neutrons held together by stellar energy. Uranium, whose energy man has learned to liberate. When a neutron strikes a uranium nucleus, it is absorbed. Under the strain of the added particle, the nucleus grows unstable and splits in two with a burst of energy, releasing more neutrons. In a mass of uranium, the neutrons of one fission travel on to produce further fissions, liberating more and more energy in an intense chain reaction. This same energy will eventually light our cities, run our factories, and power our ships and planes but to harness it man must build atomic reactors."} assumed a significance rivaling that of oil. Alongside the rise in the price of uranium compared to the beginning of the Ukraine war, the competition among great powers to source uranium, to build atomic reactors or forbid non-aligned States or State actors from building atomic reactors, harnessing nuclear power, controlling liberated stellar energy or otherwise capitalizing on the physics of energy, intensified sharply. \newline \indent The Ukraine war acerbated the rising price of uranium like no prior event in the history of the element. In the years prior to the outbreak of the SARS-CoV-2, the price for uranium remained relatively low. The price of the uranium, used in nuclear power stations to generate electricity, rose by 14 per cent from the range of 24 to 26 to 27 dollars after the virus began to cause closures at the mines in Canada, Kazakhstan, and Nimibia. More than a month before Russia's full-scale invasion, the price of uranium jumped to 45.65 dollars. Kazakhstan, the world's largest producer of uranium, supplies more than 40 per cent of global demand through state-controlled Kazatomprom. Akin to the position of OPEC plus for Brent crude, Kazakhstan dominates uranium. In the days leading up to February 24th, 2022, China cornered more than fifty per cent of Kazakhstanâ€™s market. China purchases more than half of Kazakhstanâ€™s output. Since the major export route passes by rail through the Almaty region, the clashes there slowed exports, causing the price to rise.\footnote{In the last decade, China has accumulated vast reserves of uranium with a supply equivalent to 11-12 years of demand.} Without any mention of AI, data centers or sources of electricity, the Financial Times mentioned how uranium is essential for â€œthe electrification of the global economy, with nuclear energy seen as reliable source of low carbon power.â€\footnote{It is important to mention that In a famous remark about the â€œgiant fusion reactor in the sky,â€ Elon Musk has criticized nuclear energy, claiming solar power to provide an equivalent amount of power, yet harnessed from the Sun. In a tweet on December 14th, 2025, he stated: "The Sun is an enormous, free fusion reactor in the sky." Calling them "pet science projects," Musk denigrated the push for building nuclear reactors. In an earlier interview, Musk explains in an interview the amount of electricity a solar park generates is roughly equivalent to that of a nuclear reactor. Muskâ€™s point may sound like a minor technicality but against the backdrop of the rising price of uranium, the comment assumes a conspiratorial overtone. Is the emphasis on uranium merely a way to generate monies or profit for mines, investors, or finance capital? Is it a pet science project that the great powers are building or a lucrative hobby horse?} \newline \indent Launched on February 24th, 2022, the Ukraine war immediately cast doubt over the supply of uranium and its enrichment, causing prices for the precious metal to soar. Russia, the largest builder of nuclear power plants globally, is responsible for more than two-fifths of active worldwide enrichment capacity. With sanctions threatening Russia's economy, the specter of Russia's removal from the global nuclear fuel chain became a source of disruption and price volatility. The result price became 63.80 in 2022. The imposition of sanctions on Russia followed Congressâ€™ renewal of a ban on the purchase of Russian enriched uranium imports to the U.S., the observance of which hardly applied, raised the price of uranium together with the war. The war and the reaction to the war thus augmented the price immensely. Shortly after the fall of Bakhmut-Artemovsk on May 23rd, 2023, Niger witnessed a coup. The coup hastened fears over the global supply of uranium.  A major supplier to the EU, Niger sells a quarter of its uranium to Europe. In September 2023, the price of uranium surged to its highest level in 12 years. In a global renaissance of nuclear power, the exploitation of uranium for the assertion of great power caused a further rise in the price of uranium. Continuing the momentum of 2023, the price of uranium rose to 91 per pound level. By February, prices reached 105.91 dollars, marking a nearly two decade high. In 2024, the Ukraine witnessed its third anniversary, where much the fighting whittled down from heavily mechanized spearheads thrusting across great distances such as in the beginning of the war or in Ukraineâ€™s successful Kharkiv offensive to largely positional attritional warfare in a positive territorial stalemate for Russia. Against the backdrop of uncertainty in Africa with Nigerâ€™s request for American withdrawal from the country, the price of uranium continued glisten on the outward rays of the conflicts on Ukraineâ€™s horizon. Towards the end of 2024, Russia imposed its on negative export controls on uranium, crippling supply for the largest importer of Russian enriched uranium. In 2025, prices largely stabilized around 82 dollars. \footnote{ ["Uranium bucks weak commodity trend," \emph{Financial Times}.],  ["Uranium prices jump as Kazakhstan upheaval stokes supply concerns," \emph{Financial Times}. The struggle for â€œthe subjection of the world-embracing economic system to the profit interests of the bourgeoisie of each countryâ€ to become the worldâ€™s superpower leads inevitably to â€œbarbarous disorganization and chaos,â€ â€œa ceaseless struggle for new and ever new fields of capitalist exploitation, which must be obtained from the one and same source, the earth.â€ The supply of uranium thus concentrated in only a few countries with the enrichment process equally concentrated in Russia, demonstrates how intractable the global economy to singular dominion truly is.}

\entry{Wooldbridge, Michael} {} {} {Michael Wooldbridge is one of the founders of Artificial Intelligence who distinguishes himself from contemporaries like Eric Schmidt, an AI extremist, by his firm grasp on the limits of AI. Whereas many like Eric Schmidt attribute consciousness to machines, Wooldbridge does not. Wooldbridge, for instance, does not believe that the latest version of ChatGPT reasons. He believes that the responses ChatGPT produces are not a reflection of reason but pattern recognition. The ChatGPT machine is able to mimic the responses of the large body of data. \newline \indent The problem with Artificial Intelligence is not necessarily the data but the first principles upon which builders rely to create machines like ChatGPT. The widespread reliance on a binary number system is responsible for the limitations of its logic. The binary number system lends itself to a logic where the primary mode of evaluation is nothing but a single choice: either the unit or its negation. Logic like propositional logic is precisely the type of logic that relies on the same. In a situation where there is no middle term, the limited logic of the machine cannot progress syllogistically. In the absence of a syllogistic type of logic, the ability to move from a minor to a major premise does not happen. Hence the machine's first principles are responsible for its inability to reason. Succinctly put, ChatGPT cannot reason for lack of a middle term. \newline \indent A machine whose logic avoids Leibniz' binary number system logic\footnote{In an interview at AI's Next Frontier, Geoffrey Hinton advanced the hypothesis that mathematics is a closed system like chess; he further claim that since AI play chess, AI can play mathematics. He further claimed that "I think that AI will get much better at mathematics than people, maybe in the next 10 years or so." Hinton's assertion is highly reductive. There is nothing closed about mathematics. You can try to reduce mathematics to a closed system but Godel's incompleteness theorem obliterate the idea of "closedness." Hinton's statement is tantamount to Hilbert's program. Godel completely disabled the project to find a complete and consistent set of axioms for all mathematics. Godel's theorems prove its impossibility. GÃ¶del's incompleteness theory proceeds on the basis of two theorems. The first says that in any sufficiently complex mathematical system, there are true statements that cannot be proven within that system.  Lobachevsky's substitution of Euclid's fifth postulate for his own is an example. Like in Euclid's own system, no consistent set of axioms can be both complete and capable of proving all truths about geometry. The second theorem asserts that such a system cannot prove its own consistency. Euclidâ€™s system cannot guarantee the deductive logic of truths subsequent to the axiomatization of the fifth postulate. The insistence on a set theoretic approach to thinking about mathematics is simultaneously a blessing and curse; a blessing for its brevity, expressiveness, and convenience; a curse for its confinement of the mind to the species of modus ponens and their genera. This is set theory, propositional logic, and the Principia Mathematica overthrowing intuitive, progressive, unified consciousness. The major way forward in AI is to find a way to dispense with Leibniz's binary system of 1s and 0s to a new way of counting; a logic with rules other than those in propositional logic with rules such as modus ponens, modus tollens, hypothetical syllogisms, disjunctive syllogisms, constructive dilemmas, conjunctions, absorption, simplification, or addition must give way to a new way of computing.} can be based on James Clark Maxwell's understanding of colors. In Maxwell's systems, there are three primary colors, Red, Green, and Blue. In much the same way that the Chinese have utilized DNA to record information on cassette tapes\footnote{In an article under the title, "A compact cassette tape for DNA-based data storage," published on September 10th, 2025 in \emph{Science Advances}, a team of Chinese scientists, who are far more productive than Americans, produced the first ever DNA-based data storage on a number system unrelated to Leibniz' binary number system. Americans could never achieved such a thing because America's police state bureaucracy, of which the Socialist Equality Party is an essential component, seeks to undermine its own citizens by transforming political dissidents into targets the Federal government exploits for the sake of laundering hundreds of millions of dollars on "investigations." America's insistence on wastefulness is extremely advanced, since the Federal government's police state organizations such as the Socialist Equality Party have infiltrated American universities with the a fellow police state organization, the United Auto Workers union. The UAW fulfills the function of an Orwellian thought police on graduate students so that laboratories in Computer Science, Artificial Intelligence, or Information Technology never benefit from the talented appreciation free thinking graduate students are entitled to enjoy in a true democracy. The money that America must spend on agents from the UAW to police graduate students is wasted on non-productive surveillance.}, the three colors, whose unity is white, produce four terms. A fifth term may be the deprivation of the four. A Maxwellian type of color-based storage could easily meet or exceed the storage power of DNA, since marking for DNA consumes more space on a ribbon in a cassette than color. Color on film would easily store far more than DNA on a cassette's ribbon, just as GAF viewers such as the "Pana-Vue 1" or "ViewMaster" demonstrate. Hence even in the area of data storage, which the repudiation of Leibniz' binary number system has already confirmed the extensibility of a non-binary system, Maxwell's color system may provide for greater computational power (being able not only to compute but to store information) than preceding types of computational systems.

\entry{Yemen} {} {} {During the third anniversary of the Ukraine war, Al-Jazeera published a post with a video no longer than 17 minutes on X. In the video the Qatari news channel described the first proxy war in the Middle East.\footnote{\textarabic{"Ø£ÙˆÙ„ Ø­Ø±Ø¨ Ø¨Ø§Ù„ÙˆÙƒØ§Ù„Ø© ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù„Ø´Ø±Ù‚ Ø§Ù„Ø£ÙˆØ³Ø·".. #Ø§Ù„Ù…ØªØ­Ø±ÙŠ ÙŠÙƒØ´Ù Ø¬Ø°ÙˆØ± Ø§Ù‡ØªÙ…Ø§Ù… Ø¥Ø³Ø±Ø§Ø¦ÙŠÙ„ Ø¨Ø§Ù„ÙŠÙ…Ù† ÙˆØ³Ø¹ÙŠÙ‡Ø§ Ø£Ù„Ø§ ÙŠÙƒÙˆÙ† Ø§Ù„Ø¨Ø­Ø± Ø§Ù„Ø£Ø­Ù…Ø± Ø¨Ø­ÙŠØ±Ø© Ø¹Ø±Ø¨ÙŠØ©ØŒ ÙˆÙƒÙŠÙ ØªØ­ÙˆÙ‘Ù„ Ø¨Ø§Ø¨ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ù†Ø¯Ø¨ Ø¥Ù„Ù‰ ÙˆØ§Ø¬Ù‡Ø© Ø¨Ø¯Ù„Ù‹Ø§ Ù…Ù† Ø´Ø¨Ù‡ Ø¬Ø²ÙŠØ±Ø© Ø³ÙŠÙ†Ø§Ø¡} [AJArabic:2009598633453482113]}  The video picks up right in the middle of Great Britain's occupation of Yemen when on the December 10th, 1963 the so-called Aden Emergency erupted. The video's first document is from April 22nd, 1964 when Great Britain decided to make contact with Israel in regard to Yemen. Penned to the SAS Squadron in Aden, the document outlines Great Britain's Secretary of State's approval for the creation of the Aden Group, a joint military intelligence group designed to coordinate Great Britain's activities with Israel for a mutually beneficial outcome for both parties. Great Britain's members joined the Aden Group from the Suez Group after Abdul Nasser nationalized the Suez Canal. Considered to be the last remaining vestage of Great Britain's Empire from the outcome of World War II, Yemen represented a number of problems for the SAS, whom the local Yemenis considered to be an occupying force. In what follows, the narrator explains how Yemen became the site of the Middle East's first proxy war with minor great powers, Israel and Egypt, funding one or more of the conflicted sides in Yemen to assert control over the country as a sphere of influence for a major power. The Egyptian army was fighting with the Yemeni republicans against the monarchists, whom the Aden Group sought to support. The Union of Soviet Socialist Republics supported Egypt; Great Britain supported one or more of the factions in Yemen.
\newline \indent The result of the Aden Group's first meeting resulted in Israel's first mission outside of its geography; Izthak Rabbin dispatched Zeev Liron, a fluent Arabic speaker, to fly undetected from Israel to Yemen for two things: 1) to confirm that a rebel tribal force in support of the Yemeni monarchy under Imam Hadr al Badr could actually fight against the Egyptians; and 2) secondly, Liron needed to confirm that the Badr intervention could be effectively executed without Egyptian interference. Based on a post unreleased operation report, Rabbin authorized the attack in support of Badr. 
\newline \indent On March 31st, 1964 a squadron of Israeli fighter jets left Israel from Israel's Tel Noof airbase south towards Yemen's Sanaa; the Israeli fighter jets were instructed to land in Djibouti, Ethiopia\footnote{The video displays a newsreel with Moshe Dayan with his famous eye patch, saying that Israel had a cooperation with Ethiopia for years and years. One of the witnesses explains how the Mossad maintained large bases in Ethiopia and Nairobi. } only to return north according to the same route. The mission focused on dropping weapons, the serial numbers of which specialists removed prior to the mission, for the sake of arming the Badr rebels with unrecognizable weapons that could not be traced back to Israel; most the weapons came from stockpiles of Nazi World War II weapons such as the heavy 81 mm mortars, such as the MG-42 machine gun, German luger 9 mm pistols, or British Enfield rifles.\newline \indent The Israelis sought to exploit the Yemeni conflict to weaken further the Egyptians, who became ever more bogged down in a fight against the Yemeni monarchists. With Egypt weakened, Israel gambled to reduce the risk of a renewed armed conflict with Egypt after the 1956 war. Weakening Egypt, however, was not the only goal. Upon the promise of a restored imamate, Badr royalist vowed to recognize the state of Israel.\newline \indent After the Egyptians lost the Sinai peninsula in 1967, the Egyptians turned south. The Egyptians were no longer able to block the Straights of Tiran due to the loss so the Egyptians sought to focus on Bab-al Mandeb where the conflict shifted. The video details how the wider implications of Israel's proxy war with Egypt in that area touched upon a more global struggle the Union of Soviet Socialist Republics raised with the West under the leadership of the United States. \newline \indent the video documents the involvement of the Palestinian Liberation Organization on an oil tanker transferring oil from Iran to Israel called the Coral Sea. \newline \indent The video ends with the Yom Kippur War on October 6th, 1973 where Egypt successfully recaptured the Suez Canal in a surprise attack, disabling Israel's ability to execute its strategy for weakening Arab control over the most important parts of the Arabian Peninsula, namely, the Suez Canal, the Straight of Tiran, Bab-al Mandeb, or the Red Sea in general.  
} 

\entry {Yevamot} {} {} {After the long series of wars Israel fought during the Ukraine war, the first of which began after the bloody October 7th terrorist attack, the Israeli community's leading intellectuals began to revisit aspects of the Jewish tradition, especially in regards to polygamy. Versed in the language, history, thought, or practice of Islam from its neighbors, some friendly, some inimical, many Israelis have begun to question whether or not the European style of marriage is the most optimal way to live a Torah-true lifestyle. Some, especially those versed in the laws of exponential growth\footnote{}, have begun to view marriage from a Malthusian perspective; if the State of Israel faces a major demographic challenge in the next few decades from the Arab birthrate, compounded by unrelenting warfare on all borders, the prospect of denying the Islamic habit, practiced extensively throughout the deserts most famously by Bedouins in the Levant, no place in Israel's own society is under fire. While women staff Israel's military, the majority of the soldiers are males; with high casualties resulting from the relentless warfare, the demand on the dwindling supply of Israeli males has made the idea of polygamy far more congenial than in years past. The ideas of Yevamot have suddenly begun to circulate in circles on social media circles with far more greater frequency than in previous years. 
}

\entry{Ypi, Dr. Lea} {} {} {Dr. Lea Ypi is one of the few female in the 21st to survive a highly predatory academia to publish a defended Ph.D. thesis upon receipt of her degree. While the modern world has accomplished a great deal on the order of female biology, the decision to treat women just like men in academia disregards these accomplishments, for a woman's biology is fundamentally different from a man's. A girl at the age of five, for instance, is considered an equal to a boy at five, when in all reality the former's biological clock runs nearly double or triple the time that a boy's clock runs; the cummulative effect is that academia, a slow, arduous, retaliatory apparatus the State weaponizes to extract life from brilliant human beings, exacts double or triple the toll on women than on men. A man may finish his academic career with a prospect for a family; a woman may finish her academic career with a prospect for menopause; the contrast cannot be underestimated, especially in the toxic climate of the West's modern academia. Despite setbacks, Ypi managed to graduate, although not without multiple additional degrees. Ypi is thus a role model for women, while academia may reflect less on her work than on reform; for faster admissions with faster graduations would significantly ameliorate the plight of the female academic. An intelligent woman should not be made to sacrifice her femininity for the sake of academia's slow, arduous, retaliatory apparatus. It should bloom with her work on a Spring schedule.\footnote{If not mentally traumatized, raped, or murdered, women have an exceptionally hard life in academia. On a faster biological clock, males in academia easily exploit female anxiety over the timeliness of their graduation to inflict pain with psychology. A delay in academia, for instance, is often double, if not triple, the impact for a woman than a man. The effect on woman can be life-alterating, to say the least.} \newline \indent In her Ph.D thesis, Ypi focuses on the so-called cosmopolitian state from the perspective of European analytics political philosophy. While describing the state\footnote{Since Hegel's \emph{Philosophy of Right}, no one can say anything about the State unless he or she says something about the \emph{Philosophy of Right}.} without any reference to any of its features\footnote{The idea of a State is a profound. In the 20th century, the Bolsheviks not only came to power on the basis of their understanding of the Russian state such as is described in Trotsky's \emph{Results and Perspectives} (1906) but dissolved into warring camps over its centralization (i.e., bureaucratic or democratic), its economy (i.e., for a New Economic Policy or forced collectivization), or its underlying role for the spread of revolution (such as in a series of countries, the most salient example of which is Germany) but in these explorations of the State a fundamental feature of the State is its contradictions, primarily in terms of Trotsky's theory of the political form of nation and state and its inherent contradiction with the ever increasingly globalized world economy. In terms of its existence alone, Trotsky wrote how "[the] nation must continue as a cultural, ideologic, and psychological fact, but its economic foundation has been pulled from under its feet" by way of war. The "objective significance of the War [World War I] is the breakdown of the present national economic centres" with the "subtitution of a world economy in its stead." The political form of nation and state proposed to solve the problem of imperialism "imperialism" was not through the "intelligent, organized cooperation of all of humanity's producers" but the exploitation of the world's economic system by the capitalist class of the victorious country," where the political form of nation and state is "transformed from a Great Power into the World Power."}, Ypi relates the state to cosmopolitianism. It is hard to understand how the cosmopolitianism of one State cannot be so strong that the cosmopolitianism of another marks a point of differentiation so prominent that the states become undoubtedly differentiated. The idea that the State may treated like a unit confounds the modern understanding of the State, for no State is created equal, equal, or equalizing. \newline \indent In terms of Ypi's later works, Ypi exhibits a common reflex in academia. The reflex is to daydream about the past. Academia bypasses the three hundred years after Kant to consider only Kant's \emph{Zum ewigen Frieden. Ein philosophischer Entwurf} from 1795 so that the scholar may close his or her eyes to the reality of contradictions Hegel's philosophy introduced forever hereafter into every aspect of modern life. The reliance on Kant's dream for a perpetual peace based on Kant's philosophy with devices like the categorical imperative make for excellent headlines but little to no substance for a resolution of the problem, for just as the categorical imperative dissolves, the dissolution of Kant's ideas of the State dissolve. The inescapability of the dissolution is as profound as the consequences of its dissolution, not just for philosophy but for the past three hundred years. These are years of the most profound warfare in mankind, the likes of which only an implementation of Hegel's philosophy unlock from the complex of contradiction.
}

\entry{Zaslon-M radar} {} {} {With the R-37M missile at their disposal, Russian MiG-31BMs equipped with the Zaslon-M radar have been able to fire at Ukrainian aircraft from very considerable distances,  since the beginning of the Ukraine war, without entering any of the areas in which the Ukrainian anti-aircraft defenses were operating. \newline \indent Nonetheless, the Zaslon-M radar, equipped on MiG-31BM interceptors, demonstrates how dependent the modern Russian war machine continues to be in its reliance upon the almost unrivaled treasure chest of discoveries, inventions or ideas the Soviet Union bequeathed its usurpers upon collapse. 

%https://www.deagel.com/Components/Zaslon/a003152

} 

\entry{Ziegler, GÃ¼nter } {} {} {Ziegler, GÃ¼nter M. together with Aigner, Martin produced a book dedicated to the most elegant demonstrations of solutions to problems in mathematics.  Published in 1998, the BOOK, as the famous mathematician, Paul ErdÅ‘s, envisioned the title, contain summarizations of proofs from books.  Grouped into five parts, number theory, geometry, analysis, combinatorics and graph theory. The book has passed through six editions from 1998 to 2014. 1st edition: Proofs from THE BOOK. Springer. 1998. ISBN 978-3-662-22345-1., 2nd edition: Proofs from THE BOOK. Springer. 2002. ISBN 978-3-540-67865-6., 3rd edition: Proofs from THE BOOK. Springer. 2004. ISBN 978-3-540-40460-6., 4th edition: Proofs from THE BOOK. Springer. 2010. ISBN 978-3-642-00855-9., 5th edition: Proofs from THE BOOK. Springer. 2014. ISBN 978-3-662-44204-3., (6th edition: Proofs from THE BOOK  Springer. 2018. ISBN 978-3-662-57264-1.] Ziegler's book is certainly a major contribution to the discussion of mathematics. \newline \indent The chapter on number theory is by far the most fascinating. It is the most fascinating for a number of reasons. The first reason is that the book presents Euclid's theorem on the infinity of prime numbers from the perspect of set theory. Euclid did not envision prime numbers in terms of sets, since sets did not exist at the time Euclid composed the \emph{Elements}. The way Euclid's thought advances is thus fundamentally different from the way set theory operates on numbers. Euclid proved the infinity of prime numbers not by way of counting, zero, one, two, or three; he did not prove his theorem on the infinity of prime numbers by reference to any number at all; Euclid proved his theorem about inifinte primes by way of reference to points, lines, and planes on givens in specific proportions. It is important to emphasize this primary difference for two reasons; the reasoning of the ancient Greeks did not proceed in terms of quantities; the idea of magnitude, the likes of which requires a stability incomptibile with ancient Greece, did not figure prominently, if at all, into the abstract objects of the ancient Greeks. The ancient Greeks thought in terms of analogy\footnote{It is alleged that Aristotle devised fourteen different ways to invoke the so-called "necessity" of a demonstration. If any discussion in the history of the science of logic ever touches upon the idea of "necessity" Aristotle invokes to certify the irreversible requirement for admission of a logical inference. The idea that an inference may result in one and only one inference is the fundamental rule of Aristotlean logic. Is the necessity by which Aristotle's fourteen laws on the syllogism equivalent to the necessity by which Euclid's demonstrations require the admission of a logical inference without alteration? Can Euclid's necessity be reduced to Aristotle's? Is there a difference in the necessity? What is necessity? Are Aristotle's or Euclid's necessity without parallel to anything else in the sciences?}; the idea of magnitude is only cognizable in terms of pairs of entities, whose relationship may be replicated or manipulated to such an extent that the property in focus shifts from one pair of compared objects such as line to that of another; in Euclid's proof of prime numbers, he makes no mention of counting at all; he mentions only a comparison of pairs of compared objects in an analogy. Elements, Book VII, Pr.31, for instance, relies less on \emph{reductio ad absurdum} than on the pairs of compared objects in an analogy. Euclid's reliance on pairs of compared objects begins with the first proposition in the seventh book; the words "lesser" or "greater" both presuppose sets of compared objects. The latter end of the proposition relies upon a new set of compared objects in an analogy: "if the number which is left never measures the one before it until a unit is left, then the original numbers are relatively prime." The idea of a prime number, for instance, is thus relational; it is not only relational in terms of points or lines in a plane; they are relational in terms of the conceptuality of the differentiated idea of a number. The fact that neither Ziegler nor Aigner make no mention of Euclid's methodology demonstrates that these mathematicians have not taken note of the profound role method has played in the Enlightenment, if not the trajectory of mathematics; still more, the authors have not conveyed the original thought processes of Euclid's own method. This is a fundamental error for a book dedicated to the elegance of proof. It is actually far worse. The idea of a symbolic approach to Euclid's proof thoroughly undermines the ancient Greece insistence on speech; the ancient Greeks believed the idea of the written word merely reflected the ideas human beings exchanged verbally; it is not merely a nuance but a reflection of Euclid's explanation of things said; it is not a reflection of Euclid's explanation of things symbolized; Euclid did not envision mathematical entity in terms of symbols. The symoblization of mathematical entities is as inimical to the provision of demonstration as diagrams. Euclid explained ideas in ordinary, everyday, ancient Greek.  \newline \indent The second problem is with infinity itself. The third reason is that the first chapter hardly discusses the idea of the infinity. While familiarization with Euclid's demonstration on the infinity of prime numbers might compel readers to imagine infinity from the opposite of the necessity in Euclid's demonstration. The development of a progressive infinity based on the impossibility of a \emph{reductio ad absurdum} undermines the moments in the cognition of an expanding idea of infinity. \newline \indent It seems odd that Paul ErdÅ‘s, who would have undoubtedly marvelled at the Dedekind \emph{Schnitt}, would not have mentioned Dedekind's famous proof, differentiating the real numbers by way of a division from the rational numbers. Dedekin's \emph{Schnitt} proceeds more like a construction than a demonstration. Dedekind's comparison of two sets thus gave rise to his understanding of a lesser compared to a greater infinity. In his definition of an infinite set, for instance, Dedekind described a set as infinite when it is "similar to a proper part of itself." The self-reflective construction of infinity thus separates contemporary number theory from ancient number theory by virtue of method but not merely in terms of the theoretical framework but within the progression from one mathematical entity to the next such that the former may be set up against the latter in a relationship. \newline \indent The absence of any discussion of Dedekind's methodology, which is easily duplicatable for extension into mathematics, is a startling omission. The fact that neither Ziegler nor Aigner make no mention of a comparison of Euclid's methodology to that of Dedekind's in terms of infinity is peculiar, since the focus of the first chapter is on infinity. It is also peculiar, since Dedekin's reliance upon points and a line in a plane recalls Euclid's theoretical framework. What is even more peculiar is that the relations between these sets, which are often described as lesser or greater, are not subjected to the transformation of a pair of compared objects in an analogy, as Dedekind's predecessor envisioned prime numbers and infinity.\footnote{If the set of rational numbers is countable but the set of real numbers is uncountable, the relation between the two ought to be 1) such that the comparison is duplicatable or else 2) the proportion itself is capable of reproduction by a pair of compared objects. The fact that one is less or the other great has not become the subject of a comparison draws into sharp relief the centrality of method for mathematics. It is not hard for a cobbler or a mechanic to see that less important for a solution is the problem itself than the way the problem itself is viewed. A cobbler may receive shoes. The most immediate response is to turn the shoe over to the sole. A mechanic receives cars. The most important view for him or her is from the bottom up. The ability to view a problem is at times more fundamental than the actual problem itself.} It is thus precisely here one would think not only an exposition of these different methods would be appropriate but necessitate a detailed exposition of their nuanced intricacies for the explanation of mathematics in general.  
}

While many in the circles of military war planners behind U.S.-led NATO's campaign for expansion of the private central banking alliance have only considered openly the revivification of Adolf Hitler's Directive 21, the inversion of Zhukov's late war campaign from east to west is one of the considerations for Moscow.}
